ciliumNetworkPolicies: resource watcher for CiliumNetworkPolicy objects\n//   - maxPerNamespace: maximum number of policies allowed per namespace (0 = unlimited)\nfunc NewPolicyQuotaController(\n\tciliumNetworkPolicies resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy],\n\tmaxPerNamespace int,\n) *PolicyQuotaController {\n\treturn &PolicyQuotaController{\n\t\tmaxPerNamespace:       maxPerNamespace,\n\t\tciliumNetworkPolicies: ciliumNetworkPolicies,\n\t\tnamespaceCounts:       make(map[string]int),\n\t\tlog:                   log,\n\t}\n}\n\n// Run starts the PolicyQuotaController loop. It processes CiliumNetworkPolicy\n// events from the resource watcher and maintains per-namespace counts.\n// Run blocks until ctx is cancelled.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) Run(ctx context.Context) {\n\tc.log.Info(\"Starting PolicyQuotaController\")\n\n\tevents := c.ciliumNetworkPolicies.Events(ctx)\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\tc.log.Info(\"Stopping PolicyQuotaController\")\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\tcase event, ok := <-events:\n\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\tc.log.Info(\"PolicyQuotaController event channel closed\")\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tswitch event.Kind {\n\t\t\tcase resource.Sync:\n\t\t\t\tc.log.Debug(\"PolicyQuotaController: initial sync complete\")\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n\n\t\t\tcase resource.Upsert:\n\t\t\t\tns := event.Object.GetNamespace()\n\t\t\t\tkey := event.Key\n\n\t\t\t\tc.mu.Lock()\n\t\t\t\t// Check if this is a new policy (not an update to existing).\n\t\t\t\t// resource.Key includes namespace/name so we track by key.\n\t\t\t\t// For simplicity we track by namespace: on upsert we always\n\t\t\t\t// increment if this is a new key. We use the store to get\n\t\t\t\t// accurate counts.\n\t\t\t\t_ = key\n\t\t\t\t_ = ns\n\t\t\t\t// Rebuild counts from current store to stay accurate.\n\t\t\t\tc.rebuildCountsLocked(ctx)\n\t\t\t\tc.mu.Unlock()\n\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n\n\t\t\tcase resource.Delete:\n\t\t\t\tc.mu.Lock()\n\t\t\t\tc.rebuildCountsLocked(ctx)\n\t\t\t\tc.mu.Unlock()\n\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// rebuildCountsLocked rebuilds the namespaceCounts map from the current store.\n// Must be called with c.mu held.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) rebuildCountsLocked(ctx context.Context) {\n\tstore, err := c.ciliumNetworkPolicies.Store(ctx)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tc.log.WithError(err).Warning(\"Failed to get CiliumNetworkPolicy store\")\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tcounts := make(map[string]int)\n\tfor _, obj := range store.List() {\n\t\tns := obj.GetNamespace()\n\t\tcounts[ns]++\n\t}\n\tc.namespaceCounts = counts\n}\n\n// CheckQuota returns an error if the namespace has exceeded the configured\n// maximum number of CiliumNetworkPolicy resources. If maxPerNamespace is 0\n// (unlimited), CheckQuota always returns nil.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {\n\tif c.maxPerNamespace == 0 {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tc.mu.RLock()\n\tcount := c.namespaceCounts[namespace]\n\tc.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tif count >= c.maxPerNamespace {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\n\t\t\t\"namespace %q has reached the CiliumNetworkPolicy quota: %d/%d policies\",\n\t\t\tnamespace, count, c.maxPerNamespace,\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// NamespaceCount returns the current number of CiliumNetworkPolicy resources\n// in the given namespace. This is safe for concurrent use.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) NamespaceCount(namespace string) int {\n\tc.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer c.mu.RUnlock()\n\treturn c.namespaceCounts[namespace]\n}\n\n// SetNamespaceCount directly sets the policy count for a namespace.\n// This is intended for testing purposes only.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) SetNamespaceCount(namespace string, count int) {\n\tc.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer c.mu.Unlock()\n\tc.namespaceCounts[namespace] = count\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1631,"cache_read_input_tokens":45566,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":1631,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":18,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"381ec67a-4490-49af-a189-e087c9a7f2dc","uuid":"ca478187-c62d-4b62-8fe9-94131b10ee67"}

ciliumNetworkPolicies: resource watcher for CiliumNetworkPolicy objects\n//   - maxPerNamespace: maximum number of policies allowed per namespace (0 = unlimited)\nfunc NewPolicyQuotaController(\n\tciliumNetworkPolicies resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy],\n\tmaxPerNamespace int,\n) *PolicyQuotaController {\n\treturn &PolicyQuotaController{\n\t\tmaxPerNamespace:       maxPerNamespace,\n\t\tciliumNetworkPolicies: ciliumNetworkPolicies,\n\t\tnamespaceCounts:       make(map[string]int),\n\t\tlog:                   log,\n\t}\n}\n\n// Run starts the PolicyQuotaController loop. It processes CiliumNetworkPolicy\n// events from the resource watcher and maintains per-namespace counts.\n// Run blocks until ctx is cancelled.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) Run(ctx context.Context) {\n\tc.log.Info(\"Starting PolicyQuotaController\")\n\n\tevents := c.ciliumNetworkPolicies.Events(ctx)\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\tc.log.Info(\"Stopping PolicyQuotaController\")\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\tcase event, ok := <-events:\n\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\tc.log.Info(\"PolicyQuotaController event channel closed\")\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tswitch event.Kind {\n\t\t\tcase resource.Sync:\n\t\t\t\tc.log.Debug(\"PolicyQuotaController: initial sync complete\")\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n\n\t\t\tcase resource.Upsert:\n\t\t\t\tc.mu.Lock()\n\t\t\t\tc.rebuildCountsLocked(ctx)\n\t\t\t\tc.mu.Unlock()\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n\n\t\t\tcase resource.Delete:\n\t\t\t\tc.mu.Lock()\n\t\t\t\tc.rebuildCountsLocked(ctx)\n\t\t\t\tc.mu.Unlock()\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// rebuildCountsLocked rebuilds the namespaceCounts map from the current store.\n// Must be called with c.mu held.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) rebuildCountsLocked(ctx context.Context) {\n\tstore, err := c.ciliumNetworkPolicies.Store(ctx)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tc.log.WithError(err).Warning(\"Failed to get CiliumNetworkPolicy store\")\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tcounts := make(map[string]int)\n\tfor _, obj := range store.List() {\n\t\tns := obj.GetNamespace()\n\t\tcounts[ns]++\n\t}\n\tc.namespaceCounts = counts\n}\n\n// CheckQuota returns an error if the namespace has exceeded the configured\n// maximum number of CiliumNetworkPolicy resources. If maxPerNamespace is 0\n// (unlimited), CheckQuota always returns nil.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {\n\tif c.maxPerNamespace == 0 {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tc.mu.RLock()\n\tcount := c.namespaceCounts[namespace]\n\tc.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tif count >= c.maxPerNamespace {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\n\t\t\t\"namespace %q has reached the CiliumNetworkPolicy quota: %d/%d policies\",\n\t\t\tnamespace, count, c.maxPerNamespace,\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// NamespaceCount returns the current number of CiliumNetworkPolicy resources\n// in the given namespace. This is safe for concurrent use.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) NamespaceCount(namespace string) int {\n\tc.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer c.mu.RUnlock()\n\treturn c.namespaceCounts[namespace]\n}\n\n// SetNamespaceCount directly sets the policy count for a namespace.\n// This is intended for testing purposes only.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) SetNamespaceCount(namespace string, count int) {\n\tc.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer c.mu.Unlock()\n\tc.namespaceCounts[namespace] = count\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":143,"cache_read_input_tokens":51892,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":143,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":8,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"381ec67a-4490-49af-a189-e087c9a7f2dc","uuid":"73b05eff-8526-4b45-a123-cbab7bfc8c32"}

ciliumNetworkPolicies: resource watcher for CiliumNetworkPolicy objects\n//   - maxPerNamespace: maximum number of policies allowed per namespace (0 = unlimited)\nfunc NewPolicyQuotaController(\n\tciliumNetworkPolicies resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy],\n\tmaxPerNamespace int,\n) *PolicyQuotaController {\n\treturn &PolicyQuotaController{\n\t\tmaxPerNamespace:       maxPerNamespace,\n\t\tciliumNetworkPolicies: ciliumNetworkPolicies,\n\t\tnamespaceCounts:       make(map[string]int),\n\t\tlog:                   log,\n\t}\n}\n\n// Run starts the PolicyQuotaController loop. It processes CiliumNetworkPolicy\n// events from the resource watcher and maintains per-namespace counts.\n// Run blocks until ctx is cancelled.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) Run(ctx context.Context) {\n\tc.log.Info(\"Starting PolicyQuotaController\")\n\n\tevents := c.ciliumNetworkPolicies.Events(ctx)\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\tc.log.Info(\"Stopping PolicyQuotaController\")\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\tcase event, ok := <-events:\n\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\tc.log.Info(\"PolicyQuotaController event channel closed\")\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tswitch event.Kind {\n\t\t\tcase resource.Sync:\n\t\t\t\tc.log.Debug(\"PolicyQuotaController: initial sync complete\")\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n\n\t\t\tcase resource.Upsert:\n\t\t\t\tc.mu.Lock()\n\t\t\t\tc.rebuildCountsLocked(ctx)\n\t\t\t\tc.mu.Unlock()\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n\n\t\t\tcase resource.Delete:\n\t\t\t\tc.mu.Lock()\n\t\t\t\tc.rebuildCountsLocked(ctx)\n\t\t\t\tc.mu.Unlock()\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// rebuildCountsLocked rebuilds the namespaceCounts map from the current store.\n// Must be called with c.mu held.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) rebuildCountsLocked(ctx context.Context) {\n\tstore, err := c.ciliumNetworkPolicies.Store(ctx)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tc.log.WithError(err).Warning(\"Failed to get CiliumNetworkPolicy store\")\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tcounts := make(map[string]int)\n\tfor _, obj := range store.List() {\n\t\tns := obj.GetNamespace()\n\t\tcounts[ns]++\n\t}\n\tc.namespaceCounts = counts\n}\n\n// CheckQuota returns an error if the namespace has exceeded the configured\n// maximum number of CiliumNetworkPolicy resources. If maxPerNamespace is 0\n// (unlimited), CheckQuota always returns nil.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {\n\tif c.maxPerNamespace == 0 {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tc.mu.RLock()\n\tcount := c.namespaceCounts[namespace]\n\tc.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tif count >= c.maxPerNamespace {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\n\t\t\t\"namespace %q has reached the CiliumNetworkPolicy quota: %d/%d policies\",\n\t\t\tnamespace, count, c.maxPerNamespace,\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// NamespaceCount returns the current number of CiliumNetworkPolicy resources\n// in the given namespace. This is safe for concurrent use.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) NamespaceCount(namespace string) int {\n\tc.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer c.mu.RUnlock()\n\treturn c.namespaceCounts[namespace]\n}\n\n// SetNamespaceCount directly sets the policy count for a namespace.\n// This is intended for testing purposes only.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) SetNamespaceCount(namespace string, count int) {\n\tc.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer c.mu.Unlock()\n\tc.namespaceCounts[namespace] = count\n}\n","numLines":153,"startLine":1,"totalLines":153}}}
